Frequency:                     
 
540 kHz
Beam Width:   
 
 
6° conical (2-way)
Pulse Length:   
 
 
12 microseconds
Transmit Power:  
 
 
< 213 dB @ 1 meter
Bandwidth:  
 
 
 
< 200 kHz
Maximum Range:  
 
 
100 m (328 ft) @ >= 18VDC Input Voltage
Minimum Range:  
 
 
0.5 m (1.65 ft)
Range Resolution:  
 
 
1.5 cm (0.6 in)
Ping Rate:  
 
 
 
1.0 to 5.0 Hertz
Communication Protocol:  
 
Isolated RS232 @ 4800 to 38400 bps
Serial Format:   
 
 
NMEA 0183
Synchronization: 
 
 
 1 Isolated TTL Input
Power Supply:  
 
 
11.5VDC to 20VDC - 500 mA peak, 25 mA average. (~0.5 Watts)
Isolator Input Voltage:  
 
3.3VDC to 5.1VDC at ~6mA
Maximum Operating Depth:  
300 meters (985 feet)
Temperature:   
 
 
Operating (-40°C to 60°C) Storage(-50°C to 80°C)

69.2 mm x 38.1 mm x 16.0 mm ( 2.725" x 1.5" x 0.629" )
Transducer Dimensions:

ECHO
Sea Scan
Key Features:
• Designed for Small AUV’s
• Ultra Compact Design
• Minimal Power Consumption
• Fast Simple Installation
• 100% Made in the U.S.A
• Budget Conscious Pricing
Sea Scan ECHO
This micro-miniature altimeter 
echo sounder was designed for 
use in small AUV’s, but don’t think 
just because its small in size that its 
not packed with everything you 
would expect from standard   
altimeter packages and more!
With a maximum range of 100 meters and a 300 meter depth rating 
the Sea Scan Echo is ready to go. Its shielded design and filtering 
capability minimize noise effect to maximize system performance. 
Shipped fully terminated and tested to ready to run out of the box.
The Sea Scan Echo communicates with the host computer over an RS-232 serial connection in NMEA 
0183 format using standard ASCII Characters. In Auto Trigger mode the Sea Scan Echo can operate 
independently from its host system or you can allow it to sync with your sonar. The sonar will then wait 
for the Sync input and ping rate timer to initiate data collection at rates up to 5 Hertz.
